FACILITY   (SYNCH,3CPRIHP) The Back-n white neutron source at     3280400100032 
            China Spallation Neutron Source (CSNS)                3280400100033 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) The neutrons were produced by double bunched   3280400100034 
           proton beam (1.6 GeV, ~20 kW) bombarding a tungsten    3280400100035 
           target. The neutron flux was about 3.5E6 n/cm2s.       3280400100036 
SAMPLE     Two enriched (90%) 10B samples were 5.0 cm in          3280400100037 
           diameter, evaporated on an aluminum foil 50 um in      3280400100038 
           thickness. Each sample was 82.59 and 85.05 ug/cm2 in   3280400100039 
           thickness, respectively.                               3280400100040 
DETECTOR   (SI,IOCH) The charged particles were detected by the   3280400100041 
           Light-charged Particle Detector Array system, which    3280400100042 
           mainly consisted of a silicon detector array and a     3280400100043 
           vacuum chamber. 15 rectangular (2.0 x 2.5 cm2)         3280400100044 
           silicon detectors with 500 um in thickness could       3280400100045 
           cover the emission angle of the particles from 19.2    3280400100046 
           to 160.8 deg. The distance between the center of the   3280400100047 
           silicon detector and that of the 10B sample was 20.0   3280400100048 
           cm. A gridded ionization chamber (GIC) and three       3280400100049 
           delta E-E detectors were installed and tested.         3280400100050 
METHOD     (TOF) The neutron energy was determined by TOF         3280400100051 
           method, the length of the flight path was 57.99 m.     3280400100052 
           The events were measured in turns, about 16 h for      3280400100053 
           measurement foreground and about 8 h measurement for   3280400100054 
           background for each turn. The total beam duration was  3280400100055 
           about 357 h.                                           3280400100056 
MONITOR    (5-B-10(N,A)3-LI-7,,SIG) The measured cross sections   3280400100057 
           were normalized according to standard cross section    3280400100058 
           from ENDF/B-VIII.0 in 0.3-0.5 MeV region.              3280400100059 
           (92-U-235(N,F),,SIG) neutron spectrum shape            3280400100060 
           determination.                                         3280400100061 
MONIT-REF  (,,3,ENDF/B-VIII.0,525,2018)                           3280400100062
